< Review>
Me and my family brought 5 of our other family members who just came visit us from Taiwan, all of us were very satisfied with the quality of the foods there. My wife said that the rice box is even better than the one we had the most in Taipei. My youngest sister said the cold noodle she ordered was surprisingly tasty. All of us ordered different kind of dishes and we all loved it. We will definitely come again when we are nearby.

The restaurant declared they put no MSG and any artificial additives into their foods, they also cook their food with purified water. Those are the ones I concern the most, and I never had such a good experience with a Taiwanese restaurant around Rowland Heights and Irvine area, where I just moved to about half a year ago. It is not too salty, not too oily, but tastes GOOD! Also the dining environment is comfortable, I would say among most of the other Chinese restaurants around RH and Irvine I had before.

Try it once and you will know how good and healthy Taiwanese foods can be.<//Review>

<review>What a disappointment!  Should have turned and left when I saw how out of place this restaurant was in a plaza occupied by Trader Joe's.  But, then again, out of place restaurants usually have the best food (at least from my experience).  Why Thirsty, however, isn't one of these places.

To start, if you can't read Chinese, don't EVEN bother showing up to this place.  It's the first Asian restaurant I've been to that have menus that's ALL in Chinese!  Thank God I went to Chinese School!

I ordered the Beef Noodle and it was MEH.  The beef wasn't that tender and the noodle/broth was fairly typical.  I tried the pork chop and it wasn't anything special either.  I've definitely experienced better.

Overall, I was disappointed.  I thought it would be pretty good since it was rated 4 stars on Yelp and there seems to be a never ending line of people wanting to get a table.  Maybe I'm missing something they're aware of?< /review><time>1395871567084<//time></record>

He has been doing great with medication since then. My cat's prescription weight loss food is also expensive, but has provided great nutrients for his older age and he successfully lost what he needed over a year period. My cat recently became ill and they were compassionate in my worries and accommodating that I preferred to treat from home. Though he eventually needed to be hospitalized, he returned diagnosed and treated. The front staff has always been friendly and helpful with our needs, even when managing the busiest hours. <Rate>5<//Rate><Text>I can't fully put into words how much I love this clinic. I've been bringing my pets to IHAC for over a decade and have never had a negative experience. When you walk into their lobby, you'll see hand written letters and even newspaper clippings that congratulate and thank the staff for all their hard work. And the atmosphere is always welcoming!

When one of my dogs passed away, Dr John kept the clinic open after hours so that we could cremate her with as little stress as possible. They even sent us a card to express their condolences. The fact that they would go out of their way to personally send me something has only solidified my loyalty to IHAC.

I currently have two dogs, and one of them has chronic allergy issues. We tried taking him to specialists all over OC, but no matter what we tried he wasn't getting better. A single appointment with Dr John had him put on a medication that cleared the issues up almost overnight! My dog also had issues with both ACLs in his knees. The surgery was expensive, but Dr John worked with my family to formulate a payment plan. We were encouraged to bring my dog in at any point in time during his recovery, and they even crated him a few times a week to make sure he was under observation when no one was home to watch him. Not once did I ever feel anxious while he wasn't at home--the staff are so incredibly gentle, and were careful of his needs.

They offer a grooming service once a week, and she's the only groomer I trust for my dog who now has difficulty getting up and off of high surfaces due to weak back legs. They are ALWAYS careful to pick him up and place him back down, and have extra staff ensure he doesn't slip off the grooming table while he's receiving a trim. And my dog loves them! He'll gladly follow them to the back room without looking to me even once.

Despite being a small, family owned clinic, IHAC has several services to offer, and can perform surgery on the spot if needed. They also perform chiropractic treatment, dental, and even acupuncture. I never have to take my dogs to outside specialists or to other vets to get a second opinion. Issues are identified right on the spot, and taken care of almost always during the same visit. They also offer vaccines at a discount on a specific day of the week--you can get your pups up to date in a matter of minutes, with no fuss and no waiting for the vet to get to your room. It's especially nice if you have a dog who's a bit anxious while visiting.

You'll never regret giving IHAC a chance.<//Text><Pictures>None<//Pictures><response>None< /response>< gmap_id>

< text>
If you care about your pets, I'd recommend NOT taking them here.  Dr. Adams (senior) appears to only care about getting as much out of you wallet as he can, not about the well being of your pet.

Our cat suddenly became sick and we took her in.  We were told that she was dehydrated and they wanted to keep her overnight to give her an i.v. and to observe her.  That night turned into three, and every day we were told that she wasn't getting better, but if she stayed a little longer she'd recover.  On the fourth day they let us know she was about to die and we should come in.  She was gone before we could even make it to the office.  We were completely strung along so they could keep charging us for keeping our cat, while if the vet had been more honest with us we would have taken our cat home and let her pass in a more comfortable environment (or put her to sleep sooner so she wouldn't have to suffer).

Unfortunately, we gave this vet the benefit of the doubt about our cat that passed in their care and took our other cat there when it had what appeared to be a simple UTI.  After two weeks of antibiotics we were told to come in for a follow-up checkup, which became a chance to charge us for another set of tests (the cat appeared fine at this point).  The vets office was unresponsive to our calls for the test results, and when they finally talked to us about it we were treated to a simple "looks better, keep giving antibiotics, bye" as the vet rushed off.  Another week passed and our cat began to act ill again, albeit in a different way.  Took him back to be looked at and were told they have no idea what is wrong, get x-rays and bloodwork done for another $300 to find out.  When we asked the vet for more information as to what "could" be wrong, he basically shrugged and said if he knew he wouldn't recommend tests. We discussed that we can't afford this, and the vet pretty much just walked away; no discussion of why it was a good idea, no discussion of payment plans or possible price reductions.  This was typical of the vets demeanor every time we saw him, little to no discussion of why they needed to do what they were recommending, or what could be wrong with the pet.  As we left we were told we owed another $100 for the visit (where the vet spent 3 minutes with the cat and told us nothing) and the 2nd urine test (which we lead to believe was covered under the cost of the first urine test).  This was the final straw for us and have started going to a different vet.</text>

< text>
Customer Service Fair

What I like about Howard's is that their representatives are knowledgeable        about everything in their store.   What I liked about Michael is that he shows you how each feature  of an appliance works.  You do not get this kind of attention or knowledge from the sales forces at Lowe's, Home Depot, etc.  It's because I got this attention that I decided to give Howard's my business.  Delivery and installation was easy breezy.  Many people today in retail do not know what they have in their store, nor can they tell you anything about it.  I like to be  educated. I am a happy camper with the refrigerator, washer and dryer.  The third installation of my oven hood did not go as well.  The requisition of the installation was not received by Howards' subcontractor, (Longs) so the installation did not happen on the day it was supposed to.  When Longs did not call to tell me when they were coming, I knew something was wrong. When the subcontractor arrived the next day he spent 2-1/2 hrs trying to install my oven hood and finally said there was a manufacturer's defect of the product.  The next day another installer came with another hood and was able to install it.   This simple process ended up wasting 3 of my days.  Plus Michael did not tell me about an installation fee. I thought this was all included.   I initially gave a 5 star review but for these reasons I downgraded them to 3 stars.<//text>

I asked if they could ship out the one medication and express ship as they have taken so long to fill my order with no communication, they declined and told me I would have to pay for it. I asked to speak to a manager, I was told they were on lunch at 1:30pm, a week later, still no phone call from a manager. I am convinced they don't have a manager on site, or they don't care. Needless to say, my horse ran out of medication, and it was a medication you can not skip, and despite their "policy" of filling orders within 24-48 hours, this did not happen, and they had no ability to problem solve. < Review>
I don't normally take the time to do reviews, but I feel the need to do so in this situation because it seems like these reviews misrepresent the company. I read these reviews and I almost didn't buy from them because of it, but I decided to take the chance because they were a better price than the competitors.

I ordered three 6 month packs of heartworm medicine for my dog. I did that to get the free shipping for orders over $100. They followed up later that day with an email saying they had faxed a prescription authorization to my vet's office.

Then, a day or two later they called me and said that they had heard back from my vet, and that the vet had authorized the prescription, but had only permitted my getting two 6 months packs. I was a little frustrated with this, but my frustration was with my vet office. I don't think California Pet Pharmacy could have done anything about that.

Given the reviews and the fact that they're based on the west coast, I figured it would take a while to get here, but within a couple days I received my package. Everything was as I would have hoped. They even have a cute little cat and dog printed on their box, and they have a flyer explaining how they're available to call if I need a consultation about the prescription. All in all, they were very professional and courteous, and I would order from them again.</Review>

Beware: Disingenuous business practices. Would rate zero if I could.

On three purchases, regarding the expected 24 to 72 hour delivery, the first exceeded this and took a week; the second ordered on Monday, received on Wednesday; the third was out of stock and they never called to let me know. I found out only when I called after the 72 hours had been exceeded.

The MANAGER did not know when it would be back in stock. She offered me a 30% discount if I left the order open. Based on this, I decided that I'd purchase an immediate refill at my local vet and leave this one open for future use. When it finally came, I discovered they only credited me 3% and the MANAGER insisted that was all she had promised me.

3% is 1.24 -- that's such an insignificant amount. If she TRULY had said 3%, I would have laughed, said thanks for showing me how much you value your customers, and said "CANCEL MY ORDER".

So, not only do they have horrible business practices about not following up on orders when items are out of stock, they don't stand behind their promises to customers.

NEVER AGAIN.<//text>

< name>
Dawn Smith<//name>
<date>1480697255060</date><rating>1<//rating>< text>
Ordered 2 products online and opted for expedited shipping in order to make sure I would have the meds for my dog before we ran out. After a couple of days, I called to see why I had not received a shipping confirmation. I was told that one of the products was not available in the size/Qty I ordered even though it showed in stock on the web site at the time of my order. I was told the order was held up due to this. I asked them why they didn't go ahead and ship the Rimadyl which they did have in stock and was the primary purpose of our order. I was told that this just wasn't their policy. I then reminded the customer service rep that I paid for expedited shipping and would expect that they would split the shipment and send what they had in stock like most online retailers do. I was then told that in addition to the suggested shipping time of 2 to 4 days there was also a processing time of a couple of days and if I had read the fine print I would know this.

The Rep seemed incredulous that I would expect to actually receive the product in the 2 to 4 day window suggested with the expedited shipping and that I had somehow missed the fact that they also have an order processing allowance that would need to be added on top of the shipping time. I must be a moron for assuming that paying for expedited shipping of between 2 to 4 days meant that I would receive the product in 2 to 4 days.

I asked to speak with a manager and was denied. I then suggested that if I were in their shoes, I would overnight the product since this order hadn't gone smoothly and would make some changes to their website so that the suggested shipping time would include processing. Furthermore, I suggested they may want to make sure if the website shows a product in stock, that it really is in stock.  The Rep again cited policy and that they would not be willing to overnight the product. Basically I was being told this was how they do business, they aren't interested in improving and I would just have to deal with it.

Not what I would expect from a professional business in this day and age. California Pet Pharmacy would be wise to invest in some customer service training so their reps can become more professional and better equipped to handle customer service issues effectively instead of making the customer feel like they are the enemy. Will be looking for a new supplier!<//text>
